                                                                     <td width=\"444\" style=\"padding: 10px 0px; color: #333333; font-size: 11px;\">\n                                                                          <strong>Get on board with Canada's #1 to the Sun</strong><br><br>\n                                                                          As Canada's #1 to the sun, Sunwing is the largest vertically integrated travel company with more flights to  the south than any other leisure carrier. Vacationers that choose Sunwing can look forward to experiencing the difference and choosing from the widest selection of value-added packages to suit every style and budget  with exclusive perks  to the most popular resorts across the Caribbean, Central America &amp; Mexico. Whether it's a family beach vacation, a romantic escape or a reunion of family and friends, at Sunwing Vacations we understand that your time away is as special and as unique as you are. That's why we're with you every step of the way - from the moment you book, to when you board the plane to when you are welcomed at your resort. We'll make sure your vacation is a trip you will remember for years to come. <br><br>\n                                                                          Getting to your destination should be just as enjoyable as arriving there and we're proud to include return flights with Sunwing Airlines in every vacation package we sell. With our award-winning Champagne Service, you can look forward to starting off your vacation in style with a sparkling wine toast. Featuring dishes inspired by Food Network celebrity chef, Lynn Crawford, our <a href=\"/buy-on-board.asp\" target=\"_new\">Sunwing Café</a> menu offers travellers offers an extensive buy-on-board selection of light meals and snacks. We also provide an inflight entertainment program (including first-run movies) as well as kid's backpacks with games and toys. What's more our generous complimentary 23kg free baggage allowance per passenger* makes packing for your trip hassle free.<br><br>\n                                                                          We have partnered with carefully selected hotels and resorts in the best vacation hotspots across the Caribbean, Mexico, Cuba and Central America to create exclusive concepts to suit travellers of all tastes. Designed with families in mind our Smile Resorts™ offer parents a host of exclusive perks to make their holiday budget go that little bit further including kids Stay Play and Eat FREE deals, special teen pricing, complimentary kids clubs and more. Perfect for both the young and the young at heart, our exclusive SplashWorld Resorts® include complimentary admission to an on-site or nearby waterpark as well as host of other activities for all ages. A handpicked selection of the best adults only hotels, Relax Resorts™ offer couples everything they need to unwind and celebrate each other's company - from express check-in and a welcome gift to unlimited à la carte dining and generous spa discounts.<br><br>\n                                                                          To ensure you savour every minute of your precious time away, we can even help you pre-book your excursions before you arrive.  Or, if you need last minute on how to plan your trip, our highly trained and experienced destination services representatives will be happy to assist upon your arrival. So once you've confirmed your perfect getaway, all you need to do is sit back and relax. We'll do the rest.<br><br>\n                                                                          Sunwing is the proud winner of the Consumer Choice Award for its Toronto operations for four years running. Adding onto this prestigious accolade, the tour operator's Vancouver operations just earned the Consumer Choice Award category of Best Charter Airline and Vacation Provider for the first time. The award is only bestowed upon a very select group of business owners and entrepreneurs recognized by customers for their business excellence.<br><br>\n                                                                          <span style=\"font-size:9px;\">\n                                                                          **23kg baggage allowance applies to first checked item of luggage only and cannot be shared across multiple pieces of luggage. Free checked baggage allowance is available on all routes except for domestic flights and services to the U.S.A. where a luggage fee applies.\n
